in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = _ShineLoop * _Time.y;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _RampTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _RampTex_ST.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + (-u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_22 = min(max(u_xlat16_22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#version 100

uniform 	vec4 _RampTex_ST;
uniform 	float _ShineLoop;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_WorldTransformParams;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[20];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = _ShineLoop * _Time.y;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _RampTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _RampTex_ST.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 100

#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
    precision highp float;
#else
    precision mediump float;
#endif
precision highp int;
uniform 	float _EmissSpeed;
uniform 	float _ShineLoop;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[4];
uniform 	mediump float _Emissive;
uniform 	mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
uniform 	mediump float _EmisssionScale;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MainTex;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MatMap;
uniform lowp sampler2D _RampTex;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
#define SV_Target0 gl_FragData[0]
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat10_2.xyz = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz + (-u_xlat10_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat10_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_0.www * u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + (-u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_22 = min(max(u_xlat16_22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _EmisssionScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SSSScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SSSColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DetailScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _SHScale;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHBotColor;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RimlightShadowScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _RimlightColor;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DecalMetal;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _actorscale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _FurTilling;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Metallic;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Smoothness;

	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _RimLightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MatMapMul;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHColorScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = _ShineLoop * _Time.y;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _RampTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _RampTex_ST.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + (-u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_22 = min(max(u_xlat16_22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

uniform 	float _EmissSpeed;
uniform 	float _ShineLoop;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[4];
uniform 	mediump float _Emissive;
uniform 	mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
uniform 	mediump float _EmisssionScale;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MainTex;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MatMap;
uniform lowp sampler2D _RampTex;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
#define SV_Target0 gl_FragData[0]
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat10_2.xyz = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz + (-u_xlat10_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat10_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_0.www * u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = _ShineLoop * _Time.y;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _RampTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _RampTex_ST.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + (-u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_22 = min(max(u_xlat16_22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + (-u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_22 = min(max(u_xlat16_22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = _ShineLoop * _Time.y;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _RampTex_ST.zw;

    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);

    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = _ShineLoop * _Time.y;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _RampTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _RampTex_ST.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat2.x;

    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);

    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + (-u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_22 = min(max(u_xlat16_22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 100

#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
    precision highp float;
#else
    precision mediump float;
#endif
precision highp int;
uniform 	float _EmissSpeed;
uniform 	float _ShineLoop;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[4];
uniform 	mediump float _Emissive;
uniform 	mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
uniform 	mediump float _EmisssionScale;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MainTex;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MatMap;
uniform lowp sampler2D _RampTex;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
#define SV_Target0 gl_FragData[0]
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat10_2.xyz = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz + (-u_xlat10_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat10_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_0.www * u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;

out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = _ShineLoop * _Time.y;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _RampTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _RampTex_ST.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + (-u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_22 = min(max(u_xlat16_22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = _ShineLoop * _Time.y;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _RampTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _RampTex_ST.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + (-u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_22 = min(max(u_xlat16_22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat10_2.xyz = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz + (-u_xlat10_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat10_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_0.www * u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

{
    u_xlat0.x = _ShineLoop * _Time.y;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _RampTex_ST.zw;

    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;

    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);

    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;

uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = _ShineLoop * _Time.y;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xx * _RampTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * _RampTex_ST.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 100

#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
    precision highp float;
#else
    precision mediump float;
#endif
precision highp int;
uniform 	float _EmissSpeed;
uniform 	float _ShineLoop;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[4];
uniform 	mediump float _Emissive;
uniform 	mediump float _RoughNessOffset;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
uniform 	mediump float _EmisssionScale;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MainTex;
uniform lowp sampler2D _MatMap;
uniform lowp sampler2D _RampTex;
varying highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
varying mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
#define SV_Target0 gl_FragData[0]
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
lowp vec4 u_xlat10_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
lowp vec3 u_xlat10_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat10_2.xyz = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz + (-u_xlat10_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat10_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat10_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_0.www * u_xlat10_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _FurTilling;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Metallic;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Smoothness;

#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MatMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _RampTex;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat19;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].zxy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_CameraToWorld[1].yzx * (-u_xlat1.zxy) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.zxy) * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat1.yzx) * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat2.y = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_0.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xx * u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MatMap, u_xlat16_0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + (-u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xy = vec2(_ShineLoop, _EmissSpeed) * _Time.yy;
    u_xlat19 = fract(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = sin(u_xlat2.y);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 3.14159012;
    u_xlat19 = sin(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_22 = min(max(u_xlat16_22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_RampTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.zw);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19) + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _RoughNessOffset * _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat8 * u_xlat8 + u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_4.x / u_xlat19;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat19;
    u_xlat8 = _RoughNessOffset * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * u_xlat8;
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 0.0);
    u_xlat19 = min(u_xlat19, 100.0);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * 0.100000001;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * _SpecularColor.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(_Emissive);
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
